< review>
A brand new restaurant just opened in Valley Village. What a welcome addition to an area of Laurel Canyon that very little to offer.

They. have a very interesting menu that is split in two. One side offers items that go well paired with beer, and the other side of the menu goes well with wine. Of course this is only a suggestion. I chose items from both sides to go with my chardonnay, and it worked very well.

The food is delicious! I've been to the restaurant a few times. So far I've tried the grilled salmon over kale and  quinoa. Mixed in with it were pickled onions, red grapes and toasted hazelnuts. Light. but very flavorful. They also have a refreshing, and creamy gazpacho soup. which is perfect for this hot weather. I also tried the toast with truffles and brie. This was more of a hardy dish that consisted of toasted brown bread, sauteed mushrooms and gooey melted brie. Very yummy.

The menu has a lot to choose from, including salads. chicken, hamburgers, steak and pasta. The portions were large. and the prices were reasonable.

I can't wait to go back again!</review>

<text>This motel and it's owner are gems! I have never experienced such a high level of hospitality and kindness. Upon checking in the owner was knowledgable about the local eateries and told us how much longer they would be open. He went great lengths to make sure we were taken care of. <Response>None<//Response><pictures>None<//pictures><gmap_id>0x80be49fa30881835:0x6af3b3c539a079e2<//gmap_id><rate>5<//rate><user>102427698592771999087<//user><Name>Mark Fisher</Name><time>1540234429500</time>< Text>
Not your average roadside motel. Mr. Oza, the owner, clearly takes great pride in his establishment. The rooms are very clean and the beds are comfortable. Even though the entrance fronts US-395, the rooms are set back from the road. The thick cinderblock wall construction not only cuts down almost all the road noise, it keeps the rooms cooler in the summer and warmer in winter.

There are great mountain views off the back end of the hotel and a nice shaded deck and lawn area koi opposite the rooms. It is a very relaxing place to stay.

If you're used to the corporate hotel experience this might not be your cup of tea. Then again you might find it refreshingly different, including Mr. Oza's personal touch. He doesn't just run your card and toss you a key. He obviously cares about making your stay a good one.

Perfect for sportsmen who want to get out early and come back late. For other folks in transit, it's a good midway point between Reno and the L.A. Basin.

Yes I'm a fan. Stayed here over a dozen times. Never had a problem that was not immediately addressed and resolved.</Text>

I've eaten at this restaurant since it opened. I was worried when the original couple running the place retired that the food would change. Not one bit! < text>
I was Amazingly surprised and pleased upon my arrival for the first time at Thrifty Wash.  Our brand new washer broke down after only having it for 28 days and forced me into a terrible choice.  I had the option of wearing dirty clothes and smelling or going to a public laundromat.  I was not sure which option was the worst of the two.  My early days of public laundromats could cause anyone nightmares.  I pulled up with anxiety going through my body and was extremely upset that it had come to this option.  I walked in and was floored.  My eyes went right to the immaculately kept floors.  Nice large bright tile that one of the employees was mopping to keep the glow of a wonderful place I walked into.  I almost forgot I was in a public laundromat.  I walked further into the place and it was cleaner than my own laundry set up at home.  All of the washers and dryers where clean from dirt or grime.  Yes, I did decide to check out the place and to try to find some.  I just could not believe my experience.  I had a nice chat with the lady that was taking care of the place; her name is Sandy and she gave me the owner's name and number.  I wanted to give this person a call to let him know what an excellent job he and his staff have done to make this a truly wonderful experience.  When I gave the owner a call, he was pleasant and respectful, exactly what his business represents.  This is the first review I have done for any type of business that I have patronized and it gives me great pleasure to do so.  Oh, I almost forgot, if you want a snack of chips, candy, or soda while waiting, it won't break the bank.  They are only .50 cents each...Yes..that is right!!..yes, even for soda!!..Thank you Mr. Jim Gordon and Sandy for making my day!</text>

<user_id>108386721684463126054<//user_id>< user_name>
Simon Holzman< /user_name>
< Time>
1598627431285<//Time>
< Rating>
5<//Rating>
< review>
We live in the mountains above Palm Desert where the temperature in the summer can hit 100 degrees and yet fall to 20 in the winter.

We had lived in our home for 15 years without quite being able to justify installing A/C since our Swamp Cooler coped reasonably well apart from about a month a year and we were out of the house during the days.

And then Covid hit and we were working from home and our Swamp Cooler simply couldn't do enough to make the 100 degree temperature during the day livable.

So, we asked Castillo Heating & Air Conditioning for some suggestions and a quote.

They proposed a Ductless three-way split system which would save us money on Propane during the winter months as well as cooling the house during the summer.

It took them two days to install it but they were quiet enough that we could work throughout with a minimum of disruption.

The ductless mini-split was amazing and made the temperature in the house much cooler. Indeed, my teenage daughter's room is like a morgue because she likes it really cool and keeps the door closed (did I mention "teenage").

However, the unit in the Master Bedroom was not performing as well as we would have liked. It was still acceptable to me, but my wife wasn't satisfied (I am not criticising her; she was right - I'm simply less aware of my environment than she is and didn't notice that it was closer to 80 than to the 75 it was set to). We called Castillo two times to look at it.

The first time, there was a genuine issue. One of the two fuses in the outside unit had blown and so it was running on half power. This was better than not running at all, I suppose, but the fact that it was running meant that we didn't have any reason to check the fuses. They replaced the fuse and assured us that it was very rare for them to blow like that and it was probably just a bad fuse in the first place. In the 6 weeks since then, the fuses have been fine despite a few power outages due to our Utility.

My wife was still unhappy and called Castillo's again. The chap that came examined everything again and was helpful and polite. Finally, he noticed that the vent in the Master Bedroom for the Swamp Cooler was still open and was about 4 foot above the ductless unit in that room. By checking with his thermometer, he found that the ductless unit was effectively sucking the air from outside through that vent. This was made worse by the fact that the swamp cooler is sort of above the outside condenser and so that air was extra warm.

He closed and covered that vent (and covered the other vents as well which were doubtless leaking air despite being closed) and, sure enough, it made a HUGE difference - Instead of being 78 degrees in the Master Bedroom, it was 68 last night ! (We have now set it to 75 and it's doing great.)

Thank you Castillo's for your hard work, your patience and your kindness when you must have been thinking that we were complete pains.

Very Highly Recommended.</review>

Not premium teas and milks like Boba Guys, but it's a decent milk tea with huge serving sizes for a good price! I ordered the green milk tea with honey and lavendar flavor and added 1 topping, housemade grass jelly. Haven't tried their shaved snow or ice cream macarons yet because the macarons look a little stale in the freezer. Also it's usually too chilly and foggy in this area for frozen desserts!! But I saw that they have a stock of board games in the corner and a few tables for groups, so would love to come back to hang out.

TIP: Join the FiveStar app and sometimes they will send you a free drink! (No purchase necessary)</Review>

<user_id>103711841096201936940</user_id><username>Jason M< /username>< time>
1593043484570<//time>

< Text>
Truly horrible overall experience at the location in Sacramento on Florin! My strongest suggestion is find a car somewhere else!

My wife found a car via online search at this dealership. We went in together to look at the vehicle. Amed, who was the sales rep let us text drive the vehicle as the usual with the initial experience of any car dealership. Once we got back we negotiated. We said we were going think about it, they were pushy for the sale (typical like anywhere). Everything was seemed normal until the paperwork started.

As soon as the contracts were printed, Amed begins to multitask between us, another customer who was looking into a car, and apparently someone who he had already helped. Every question we had Amed could not answer himself. He knew nothing about the vehicle and he had to ask Reggie on several occasions about our contract. Reggie never sat down with us to explain it, he just yelled across the main floor from his desk.

Now this is were the experience took a turn for the worst. Reggie who is the floor manager, made several verbal promises that he did not deliver on or gave us the run around unnecessarily.

First, we had been assured that the car had been recently maintained which required a specific filter to be replaced ($350+ part/labor). Instead of replacing the filter, their service department just reset the "maintenance required" light and told us that everything had recently been looked at, maintained, and cleared. I guess they didn't expect us to take it to Toyota to pay for a vehicle inspection.

Second, their ad that they posted for public view online said that the car had GPS navigation installed and ready to use. When we drove off the lot, the SD Card with navigation was missing ($182 pricetag) and navigation was not working. After being instructed by a Toyota service technician that the dealership is responsible for the missing piece we informed Reggie at Integrity Autosales. He was reluctant to provide us one until my wife pulled their ad and explained what they were telling potential customers. At that point he put in a order for the SD card, it took about 2-3 weeks to receive it.

Third, Reggie promised both my wife and I without us bringing to his attention the matter of a second key FOB($500+) for the car. Now this is the main reason for me writing a review. Reggie promised my wife that they will send out the second key once the contracts are signed and approved. We have not recieved the key to this day. To make matters worse, when I questioned them about the key they said that it was shipped via mail with the SD card (which we received with no key FOB in it). The package that came was not tampered with and was in a paper thin UPS next day air envelope.

So I then follow up with them, I am put in touch with a Victoria since she is the person that was responsible for mailing out the key. She immediately gives me attitude when I ask questions regarding the tracking number, when it was sent, how much the package weighed, etc. She insists on calling me back to get answers... never does. I call back 40 minutes and she has left the building.

After I decide to visit the location in person and get more direct information. Reggie greets me improperly and answers any questions I have with short one word answers. When there is no progress with our conversation, he stares at me asking me "What are you going to do about it?" I become frustrated and spout off like a crazy person.

All I hope is that this review is read by at least one person we don't share similar stories. Too much time and effort was put into this.

Please stop supporting the location!

This dealership in Sacramento is by far the worst car buying and customer service experience my wife and I have ever been put through.

Just because they say they have integrity does mean they do... we were the naive. Don't make our mistake.< /Text>

<Pics>None</Pics>< Review>
On 05/12/2018 I went to Integrity Auto Sales in Sacramento, CA to purchase a vehicle for my fiance. I took the chance with the business based off the company having decent reviews and a professional impression by the salesperson. We went with a 2015 Ford Explorer that had minor cosmetic issues (window trim) and were told the disclosed "structure damage" I was signing was in regards to that and that I would be given a "Due Bill" to bring the car back in for the window trim to be glued back down. They gave me a Carfax showing a clean history with the only noted damage being the window trim. Not being educated that structure damage meant the actual frame of the vehicle, or having the real disclosure of what it meant, we went with the vehicle in trusting that this was the case. Shortly after my fiance lost her job and, in having to pay two cars on my own, I took it into Carmax in Sacramento, CA on 09/18/2018 to possibly get into a smaller vehicle with less monthly payments. Upon their inspection of the vehicle and in pulling a full vehicle history report, Carmax found that the auction disclosed on 01/2018 to the dealership that structural/frame damage had been noted with the vehicle. We have three children that the dealership was aware of and they still put my fiance and children in an unsafe vehicle willing knowing that they were trying to hide having to disclose the actual damage within the car. I contacted the dealership the same day I received the news from Carmax and the owner Vitaly told me to bring the car in and he would trade the car in at full car value for a different vehicle. I took his word and we went into try and speak with them about possibly returning the vehicle since it was a fraudulent sale at that point being that they never actually disclosed accident damage to the frame of the car. Upon trying to work out the trade, the owner tried to have my fiance and I take a loss of 5,000 dollars that would be added to one of a couple of cars he gave for us to look at. In the end he tried to charge 24,595 dollars for a 2013 Kia Optima valued at 13,000 dollars. I notified him that I would not be scammed into spending twice what another car was worth for us to get out of an illegal sale, which at this point he refused to do anything more. The initial salesperson we bought the car from even admitted, which I have documented, that he was unaware of the disclosed damage to the vehicle and that he would have never made the sale if he was aware of it being more than the disclosed window trim. At this point we have sought legal counsel, as frame damage/accident history is the only mandated disclosure to be made by dealers in California and this business willingly withheld this from us. I am posting this lengthy review so that all others that may be considering, or already have, purchasing a vehicle from the establishment are readily aware of the owner/manager's slimy practices. They will do everything in their power, even if it is not legal, to get you into a car, unsafe or not. They have no care whatsoever for their customers and only care about making a sale. You have been warned to not make the same mistake I did and find a legitimate business for your car buying purposes.</Review>
